GT (fixed):  
\[
f(x,t)= -1.99164100804766\,x^3\;-\;1.99164100804766\,x(0.0248350833882069\,t+1)\;-\;1.99164100804766\,x\;+\;0.799842060559254\sin t.
\]
So GT is exactly a polynomial in \(x\) up to degree 3 with a linear-in-\(t\) coefficient on the \(x\) term, plus a pure \(\sin(t)\) term. No exponentials/logs/tanh/abs/max are present in GT.

Key structural requirements for any candidate to match (possibly under a domain restriction like \(x\ge 0\), etc.):
- Must produce an \(x^3\) term with constant coefficient \(-1.991641...\).
- Must produce an \(x t\) term with coefficient \(-1.991641...\cdot 0.02483508...\).
- Must produce an \(x\) term with coefficient \(-1.991641...\cdot(1+1)= -3.98328201609532\) (because GT has \(-1.9916 x( ... +1)\) and also \(-1.9916 x\)).
- Must produce a pure \(\sin(t)\) term with amplitude \(0.799842...\).
- Must not introduce any other functional dependence (e.g., \(\exp(x)\), \(\tanh(\cdot)\), \(\log(\cdot)\), \(\cos(\cdot)\) unless it can be phase-shifted into \(\sin(t)\), etc.). Any such term must be eliminable by setting its coefficient to 0.

Now check candidates:

1) \(c0\tanh(c1x+c2)+c3tx+c4x^3+c5\exp(c6\sin(c7t+c8))+c9x\).  
Can set \(c3,c4,c9\) to match \(xt,x^3,x\). But \(\tanh(\cdot)\) term cannot become a polynomial term on any plausible continuous domain unless coefficient \(c0=0\). Also \(\exp(c6\sin(\cdot))\) cannot equal a pure \(\sin(t)\) (it’s always positive and non-sinusoidal) unless \(c5=0\). With \(c0=c5=0\), there is no remaining pure \(\sin(t)\) term. So cannot match.

2) \(c0e^{c1x}+c2\cos(c3t+c4)+c5e^{c6\sin(c7x+c8t+c9)}\).  
No \(x^3\) or \(xt\) polynomial structure. Exponentials in \(x\) can’t become cubic on a domain. Not match.

3) \(c0+c1x^3\cos(c2t)+c3x+c4x^5+c5\cos(c6t+c7)\).  
The \(x^3\) coefficient depends on \(t\) via \(\cos(c2 t)\); GT’s \(x^3\) coefficient is constant. Only way is \(c1=0\) (kills \(x^3\)) or \(c2=0\) making \(\cos(0)=1\) constant; but then you can get \(x^3\) constant. However there is no \(xt\) term anywhere, so cannot match.

4) \(c0\frac{x}{c1+x^2}+c2x\max(0,c3+|x|)+c4x^3+c5e^{c6t}\cos(c7t+c8)\).  
Can set \(c4\) for \(x^3\). But no \(xt\) term. Also rational/max terms can’t be removed except by setting coefficients 0; then still no \(xt\) and no pure \(\sin(t)\) unless the last term can be made \(\sin(t)\) *without* exponential factor: would need \(c6=0\) so \(e^{0}=1\) and phase shift cosine to sine; possible for the \(\sin(t)\) part. Still missing \(xt\). Not match.

5) \(c0x^2+c1x+c2+c3x e^{c4|x|}+c5x^3+c6e^{c7t}\cos(c8t+c9)\).  
No \(xt\). Exponential-in-\(|x|\) term must be killed (set \(c3=0\)). Still no \(xt\). Not match.

No \(x^3\) term (only \(x|x|\) which is \(x^2\) with sign; cannot equal \(x^3\) on any open domain). No \(xt\). Not match.

GT Equivalence Verification (PO10)

GT: F0*sin(t) - omega0**c0*(gamma*t + c1)*x - omega0**c2*x**c3 - omega0**c4*x

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT numerical expression:** `-1.99164100804766*x**3 - 1.99164100804766*x*(0.0248350833882069*t + 1) - 1.99164100804766*x + 0.799842060559254*sin(t)`

Let me simplify the GT:
- `-1.99164100804766*x**3` → x³ term
- `-1.99164100804766*x*(0.0248350833882069*t + 1)` = `-1.99164100804766*0.0248350833882069*t*x - 1.99164100804766*x` → t·x term and x term
- `-1.99164100804766*x` → another x term
- `0.799842060559254*sin(t)` → sin(t) term

Combining: GT = **A·x³ + B·t·x + C·x + D·sin(t)**

where A ≈ -1.992, B ≈ -0.04947, C ≈ -3.983, D ≈ 0.7998

So GT has basis functions: **x³, t·x, x, sin(t)**

Now I'll check each candidate for whether it can express exactly these basis functions.

**Candidate 1:** `c0*tanh(c1*x+c2) + c3*t*x + c4*x**3 + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*t+c8)) + c9*x`
- tanh is not a polynomial in x; cannot match linear x term exactly for all x (tanh ≠ linear). But we can set c0=0 to eliminate tanh.
- With c0=0: `c3*t*x + c4*x**3 + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*t+c8)) + c9*x`
- We need sin(t) but have exp(c6*sin(c7*t+c8)). exp(sin(...)) ≠ sin(...). These are fundamentally different functions.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0*exp(c1*x) + c2*cos(c3*t+c4) + c5*exp(c6*sin(c7*x+c8*t+c9))`
- No polynomial terms in x (x³, x, t·x). exp(c1*x) with c1=0 gives constant. Cannot produce x³ or t·x terms.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `c0 + c1*x**3*cos(c2*t) + c3*x + c4*x**5 + c5*cos(c6*t+c7)`
- x³*cos(c2*t): if c2=0, this becomes c1*x³. ✓
- c3*x ✓
- c4*x**5: set c4=0 ✓
- c5*cos(c6*t+c7): with c6=1, c7=-π/2, this is c5*sin(t) ✓
- But missing t·x term. No way to generate it.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*x/(c1+x²) + c2*x*Max(0,c3+|x|) + c4*x³ + c5*exp(c6*t)*cos(c7*t+c8)`
- x/(c1+x²) is a rational function, not polynomial.
- x*Max(0,c3+|x|): for large enough c3, this is c2*x*(c3+|x|) = c2*c3*x + c2*x*|x|. x*|x| ≠ x² (it's x²·sign(x)).
- Missing t·x term.
- exp(c6*t)*cos(...): if c6=0, gives cos(c7*t+c8) which can be sin(t). But no t·x.
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `c0*x² + c1*x + c2 + c3*x*exp(c4*|x|) + c5*x³ + c6*exp(c7*t)*cos(c8*t+c9)`
- x² term present but GT has no x² (would need c0=0) ✓
- c1*x ✓, c5*x³ ✓
- c3*x*exp(c4*|x|): if c4=0, gives c3*x, another x term ✓
- c6*exp(c7*t)*cos(c8*t+c9): if c7=0, gives c6*cos(c8*t+c9) = sin(t) possible ✓
- But missing t·x term!
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

- No t·x, no x³.
Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 7:** `c0*exp(c1*x) + c2*|x| + c3 + c4*exp(c5*x)*cos(c6*t+c7) + c8*x³`

Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]
